<Review>This easy walk is a long drive to the ocean in  Western Marin County.  But, the drive is well worth it.
In spring enjoy the many varieties of wild flowers. This year especially (2019) after a long and bountiful rainy season, we identified  35+ varieties in colors ranging from lavender to orange and all the colors in between. It is mostly flat with three options to increase your walk to 3+ miles.

(Option 1)  Most of the wild flowers are on a single file trail out to the point. You can identify the start of this trail by the Flower I.D. board posted at the head of the trail. Single file is good. Take the time to stop and look. You will be rewarded. It might be windy and cool, but if there is no fog, you can stop at the end and look for migrating whales. Not wheelchair compatible.

The Lighthouse near here is being renovated, so the area can get crowded during peak times

Today we spotted a Pergrine Falcon, young elephant seals, deer and a coyote. Great place for a picnic lunch at the old Coast Guard Lifesaver station below the parking lot (option 2)  Paved but too steep for wheelchairs. Check with the visitors center on that issue.

Option 3 is a walk to a lookout which you might see elephant seals. Winter and Spring Birthing areas are closed to visitors so do not enter a closed area because you will be cited $$$. Enjoy.<//Review>< user_id>
111747657257481747820<//user_id>
< name>
Mark Bosch< /name>

<Time>1555454441242</Time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
This easy walk is a long drive to the ocean in  Western Marin County.  But, the drive is well worth it.
In spring enjoy the many varieties of wild flowers. This year especially (2019) after a long and bountiful rainy season, we identified  35+ varieties in colors ranging from lavender to orange and all the colors in between. It is mostly flat with three options to increase your walk to 3+ miles.

(Option 1)  Most of the wild flowers are on a single file trail out to the point. You can identify the start of this trail by the Flower I.D. board posted at the head of the trail. Single file is good. Take the time to stop and look. You will be rewarded. It might be windy and cool, but if there is no fog, you can stop at the end and look for migrating whales. Not wheelchair compatible.

The Lighthouse near here is being renovated, so the area can get crowded during peak times

Today we spotted a Pergrine Falcon, young elephant seals, deer and a coyote. Great place for a picnic lunch at the old Coast Guard Lifesaver station below the parking lot (option 2)  Paved but too steep for wheelchairs. Check with the visitors center on that issue.

Option 3 is a walk to a lookout which you might see elephant seals. Winter and Spring Birthing areas are closed to visitors so do not enter a closed area because you will be cited $$$. Enjoy.</Review>

<UserId.>108387862976344373340<//UserId.><gmap_id>0x8085dbe7bcfb4f45:0xa666f68c0b56dd2b< /gmap_id>< Text>
Chimney Rock is one of the very special places on Pt. Reyes.  You can see colonies of elephant seals from near here. A nice easy hike of a mile or two takes you out to the point, from where you can sometimes see whales.  But most special of all are the spectacular displays of wildflowers in the springtime.  Chimney Rock is one of the top places in Marin, coastal or otherwise, for wildflowers.</Text>

D&M D&M< /Name>
<Time>1497205740840< /Time>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< text>
My wife and I stayed at Lake Tahoe Resort in early June/17 and had dinner twice at their Echo restaurant.  Nice place, friendly staff, clean, and not a crowded set up with the tables/booths.  A good variety of food offerings.  Fair priced compared to similar restaurants in the area but the best thing is that there is no driving involved.
If you like ahi tuna steak seared and served raw you MUST have it there.  It was laid over a bed of rice cake/risotto with Asian slaw topped with thin slices of ginger.  The sauce they used over the ahi was absolutely delicious.  I always order seared ahi whenever it is on any menu but I have to say this was the absolute by far best I've ever had.  Wife had a delicious grilled chicken breast dish which she totally enjoyed.
The next night we decided to have burgers and thought we'd go to one of those restaurants nearby but then checked out the natural grass fed burgers at Echo and decided why would we go to a sports type bar restaurant when we can get better meat at a place as nice as Echo.  Fair priced and delicious burgers!!< /text>

< review>
These guys are absolutely amazing to work with. I love how organized there system is set up. Work is always perfect. Very detailed write ups and explanations. Prices are fair. <Rate>1< /Rate>< Text>
Do not go to Garage One Subaru!!!! Read below for my experience:

I spent over $7000 to replace my 2005 Subaru Outback XT engine. Seems kinda pricey, but I was desperate for my car to be fixed. When I finally got my car, Aaron (the head mechanic and owner) handed me the keys and said that the engine shortblock was complete. He also mentioned that the engine still vibrates quite a bit and they would need to do some more diagnostics to figure out that issue. They recommended changing the fuel filter, fuel pump, O2 sensor, MAF, checking for any vacuum leaks, etc... I spent over $1500 in parts and replaced each of those parts and the engine still vibrated quite a bit. Not only that, but also when I was on a road trip to Utah, my gas mileage on the highway was 18mpg and would stall every now and again.

I went to another mechanic (my trusted mechanic) and he did all of the tests and couldn't find anything. He recommended doing a compression test on each of the spark plug ports, but I denied saying "no no, it's a brand new engine, and I bet Garage One already did that when they finished" My trusted mechanic had me check with Garage One and they confirmed his suspicion. Garage One NEVER checked the compression after they rebuilt and put everything together!!!! My mechanic performed a compression test and cylinder 2 had bad compression.

I immediately took my vehicle to Garage One and they performed a compression test and discovered the same thing my mechanic found. They took the engine apart again and found that cylinder 2 had a cracked head and replaced it. My car ran amazingly after that! No vibration, no sputtering, no bad gas mileage, etc... except one thing... The engine area started smelling like burnt oil. During a routine oil change, jiffylube told me oil was seeping through the engine gaskets on the back side of the engine. Garage One did not tighten the bolts tight enough!!!!

I went back a 3rd time and had them put everything back together properly.

I honestly do not recommend Garage One. They are nice people, but in my experience they do not do a thorough job the first time. What I dislike the most about my experience was that they tried to charge me right after they "fixed" my engine when it was their fault in the first place.

Things I did not like:
1. They should have caught the busted head while replacing the shortblock the first time.
2. I came back 2 more times to have them fix their mistakes.
3. I followed their recommendation and spent $1500 on parts that were not needed at all.
4. Their office people give blanket answers to your questions and you are not allowed to speak to their mechanics about their diagnosis. That frustrated the heck out of me.
5. Expensive expensive expensive!!!! Buy the parts yourself and you will save hundreds, if not thousands of dollars on their huge markups.<//Text>

< Text>
This was a great dinner spot on the Friday night my wife and I arrived in Fairfax for the first time. It had all the qualities we were looking for, a great dinner menu, indoors seating, full bar, and a location right in the downtown area. The service was
outstanding, with Tyrone taking care to make sure we were happy and well fed, and he was very informative and knowlegeable of the menu and the specials. The food was top notch, the salmon special was perfectly cooked and incredibly flavorful, the Crab Cakes were exquisite, and the meatballs were tender and delicious. The Beet Salad could have used some more beets and less greenery, but it was also a great dish. Would definitely come back again next time we are in the area!< /Text>

<Text>My husband and I were passing through and decided to pop in for lunch as we saw they had outdoor seating and a good rating. Oy, where to start... The owner seemed to be running this operation single-handed. He's trying to host, serve and manage and it's not working out well. Times are tough with COVID, we understand. However, the execution is poor. He is running around with NO mask and handling food. Condiments are still being served in their greasy containers, not in ramekins or single-serve packets which would have been 100x more hygienic. There was also a sheet pan of cake sitting out, uncovered and half cut up right outside the bathroom. During this time, sanitation and precautionary measures should be the ultimate priority. His restaurant is definitely not following code.

Now let's talk about the food. We got the turkey bacon sandwich and the blt. The turkey sandwich was served on stale old bread which we ended up not eating. The turkey itself tasted cheap and processed. It was served with a side salad with blue cheese dressing. It was your average store bought salad mix. The dressing tasted more like a creamy garlic? No blue cheese in sight. We didn't eat it.

The blt should have just been called a tomato sandwich. There were like 2 strips of bacon?

Honestly the best part of this meal were the fries. Which I am sure came from a frozen bag.

The icing on the cake was waiting for 15 minutes for the owner/server to come back to our table so we could pay. Instead, we had to hunt him down to find him inside staring out the window.

These 2 sandwiches were definitely not worth the $34 price tag.

Needless to say, if we ever pass through Fairfax again we will give this place a pass.< /Text>< Pictures>

Have been going to Barefoot for many years, primarily for breakfast.

Cozy and great food.

They do a good job with lattes, particularly if the owner makes them.

I went to the Lodi Ulta today  because I had a gift card...never again. I can shop at any other of many  stores that sell beauty products and at cheaper prices and treat their customers better. <Rate>1</Rate>< Review>
This review is regarding the Salon only: Haircut + Highlights.

I want to first start off saying that my total price came out to $242.25.

I asked for brown and blonde highlights towards the bottom of my hair, i wanted to keep my roots black and get a blended bolyage look (my natural hair color is black and length was down to my lower back). After waiting for the highlights to kick in, i had a shampoo, conditioner, painful & rough scalp massage, toner and gloss.. it was time for the haircut and blowout.

With my hair wet, Sondra (salon manager) asked me how much would I want to cut my hair. I said "a few inches BELOW my shoulder." She then pointed to my bra line and asked "ok so about here." I replied "yes, perfect!"

10 minutes later my hair was sitting on my shoulders. I have NO idea what happened. I believe she knew she made this error, because she made comments about how hair grows back and can always be fixed but scars on the face is worse and permanent. I did not confront her on why she cut my hair so short because the entire time I felt intimidated by her strong personality. The whole time she kept herself busy by cleaning, bossing the other workers around, or saying "funny" comments to other customers. I truly believed that if i confronted her there would have been some excuse to explain she did nothing wrong. She didn't offer a discount or apology or anything. She played it off as if nothing was wrong.

What was worse was the color. Nothing came out besides the "blonde" color which looked more orange than anything. I sat there in shock, and just tried to hold back my tears so i can avoid any awkward debating with Sondra because I KNOW thats what would have happened.

The next day I woke up early, went to Walmart and bought a 3 dollar box of Revlon in a dark brown color and poured it over the orange peices. I can now live with the color, just going to have to wait a few months till my hair grows to the actual desired length that I wanted.

$242.25? NOT worth walking out for something I didn't ask for, with no nice hair color.<//Review>

< Text>
So glad we rented (last minute) from Getaway Tours. The staff was so friendly, accommodating, and helpful! Other than that it is an overall good place.</text>
